[1723] ✓ CORRECT
  Question: I am experiencing vomiting, abnormal breathing sounds, cough, and fever. What condition does this match?
  True Answer: croup
  Predicted: croup
 Croup is a common breathing disorder in infants and young children. It is characterized by high fever, cough, and abnormal breathing sounds. Your child may also be experiencing difficulty breathing, nasal congestion, and vomiting. Croup is caused by swelling around the vocal cords, which leads to difficulty breathing. It is important to seek medical attention promptly if your child is experiencing symptoms of croup. Your doctor may prescribe medication to help with breathing, and give you tips on how to care for your child at home.

[2021] ✓ CORRECT
  Question: I have these symptoms: ear pain, throat feels tight, hoarse voice, nasal congestion, coryza, fever, and cough. What do I have?
  True Answer: laryngitis
  Predicted: laryngitis
 Notes: The symptoms of laryngitis are coryza, fever, hoarse voice, and throat feels tight. The condition is caused by an infection of the head and neck. The medications that may be prescribed include antihistamines, decongestants, and pain relievers. The treatment for laryngitis is to rest the voice and drink plenty of fluids. The symptoms of laryngitis usually last for less than 14 days.

[2698] ✓ CORRECT
  Question: I have these symptoms: hand or finger pain, leg swelling, ankle swelling, knee pain, hand or finger swelling, knee swelling, joint pain, foot or toe pain, wrist pain, and foot or toe swelling. What do I have?
  True Answer: gout
  Predicted: gout
 Explanation: Gout is a type of arthritis that is caused by a buildup of uric acid in the body. The body can't process uric acid properly, which leads to the buildup of uric acid. The uric acid crystals then form in the joints, causing pain and swelling. Gout can affect any joint, but most often affects the big toe. Other joints that may be affected include the ankle, knee, wrist, and hand. Blood tests can be used to diagnose gout. Treatment

[85] ✗ WRONG
  Question: My symptoms are abnormal appearing skin, lower abdominal pain, skin growth, and skin lesion. What could this be?
  True Answer: osteochondroma
  Predicted: warts

Comment: This is warts. Parasitic skin infection is a skin condition caused by parasites and it has similar symptoms as warts. But parasitic skin infection is usually itchy and the skin growth is usually smooth. Warts are growths on the skin caused by human papillomavirus and it has symptoms of skin lesion, skin swelling, and irregular appearing scalp.  So it is different from parasitic skin infection.
